  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

      <b>“This love is worth the unsaid truths. <br/>The hidden lies.”</b>

</a><br><b>★★★★★! Black lies (stand-alone). Heiress’ world collide with enigmatic inventor Brant Sharp! Well on track to marriage, their life is turned upside down by secrets &amp; lies!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“This love is worth the unsaid truths. <br>The hidden lies.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫<br><b>“Goodbye My Lover”</b> by James Blunt captures the <b>beauty, pain, profound sadness</b> and… <b>soul-searching love</b> I feel about this story: <b>
  <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wVyggTKDcOE" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">♫ CLICK TO LISTEN ♫</a>
</b><br>♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫ ♫<br><br><b>Black Lies</b> is the story of heiress, <b>Layana Fairmont, Lana aka Lucky</b> raised in privilege by wealthy parents to become a trophy wife. But instead <b>she cashed in her inheritance</b> and made her <b>own version of the good life</b> by living well and working part time at the charity.<br><br><b>At a fundraiser</b> for her charity she meets inventor and CEO of BSX, <b>Brant Sharp</b> and is stricken by his beauty, intelligence and down-to-earth personality. They immediately <b>hit it off feeling an insane attraction and connection</b>. Once they overcome some hurdles they begin dating. <br><br><b>Life is on track</b> moving towards marriage when <b>their world come crashing down</b>. What follows is a story of <b>deceit, trust issues, selfishness, altruism, secrets, pain</b>, and… <b>LIES</b> pushing their lives into a tailspin. <br><br><i>Nothing can prepare you for Black Lies!</i> It’s a story about an <b>all-consuming LOVE for different people</b>! It’s about the <b>HOLD</b> that <b>sex and love can get over you</b>! About <b>wanting some things so fiercely</b>, you stop at nothing to obtain them and yield to nothing to hold onto them… <br><br>In the end you will ask yourself: <i>
  <b>What would I have done?</b>
</i> My answer is: <b>
  <i>The exact same thing!</i>
</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I will fight for this love. Lie for it. Steal for it. It’s worthy of that.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/BLHxBSbysb_zps26ac9023.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407363954ra/10681840.gif" alt=" photo BLHxBSbysb_zps26ac9023.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Four words to describe <b>Brant Sharp: Charismatic, noble, complex and secretive</b>.<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/BLhexBSbysb_zps96899920.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407363954ra/10681839.gif" alt=" photo BLhexBSbysb_zps96899920.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Four words to describe <b>Layana Fairmont, Lana aka Lucky: Focused, determined, loyal and secretive</b>.<br><br><b>Black Lies</b> might take you out of your comfort zone. It will likely <b>push boundaries and blur the line between right and wrong</b>. <br><br>I have read this story four times already and though I know the ending; the secrets and the lies… <b>I keep finding nuisances and depth</b>. It’s <b>unique, emotional</b>, at times excruciatingly <b>painful</b> and so <b>thought-provoking</b>! <br><br>Be sure to read the newly released extended epilogue 2 years later: <b>
  <a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2014/09/26/bonus-scene-black-lies/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Read here!</a>
</b><br><br><b>Brilliant</b> plot! <b>Captivating</b> journey! <b>Excellent</b> character development! <b>Shocking</b> twists and turns! <b>Mind-blowing</b> sex scenes! And… <b>heart-stopping</b> love! <i>Thanks Alessandra!</i> This story will stay with me! <b>6 stars!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“But I will never forget you. I will always miss you.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 5 stars<br>Sexual tension rating: 5+ stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4.5 stars<br>Plot rating: 5+ stars<br>Dialogue rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling rating: 5+ stars<br>Story ending rating: 5 stars<br>*********************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 6 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this book: Yes!<br>Would I re-read this story: Yes!<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/BLendrevxBbysb_zps854c914f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407363954ra/10681841.gif" alt=" photo BLendrevxBbysb_zps854c914f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><u>My thoughts after reading 100% of draft 2:</u><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><blockquote><b>Nothing can prepare you for:<br><br><a>BLACK LIES</a><br>By Alessandra Torre</b></blockquote>

Black Lies (stand-alone)</b><br><br><a><blockquote><i><b>“This love is worth the unsaid truths. <br>The hidden lies.”</b></i></blockquote></a><br><br><b><i>Have YOU ever WANTED something so fiercely you were willing to risk it all?</i></b><br><br><b>BLACK LIES</b> is about an all-consuming <b>LOVE for different people!</b><br><br>❤ It’s about the <b>HOLD</b> that <b>sex and love can get over us</b>!<br>❤ The <b>LENGTHS</b> we might go to <b>get what we want</b>!<br>❤ The <b>signs we might IGNORE</b> to hold on to it all!<br>❤ The <b>SECRETS we might keep</b> to protect it all!<br>❤ And the <b>LIES</b> we might <b>tell to possess it all</b>!<br><br>It’s <b>DIFFERENT! It’s beautiful, emotional, thought-provoking</b>, utterly <b>sexy</b> and... at times breathtakingly <b>painful!</b><br><br><b>Brilliant</b> plot! <b>Captivating</b> journey! <b>Excellent</b> character development! <i>Thanks Alessandra!</i> This story will stay with me! <b>5 stars!</b><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><u>My thoughts after reading 80% of draft 1:</u><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><b><br><a>MYSTERY PROJECT</a><br>By Alessandra Torre</b><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20NIck%20Nacks/safexbysb_zpsbf1f7a5a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402820311ra/9990152.gif" alt=" photo safexbysb_zpsbf1f7a5a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>There are several things I have learned since reading my first Alessandra Torre book nearly 2 years ago; She is not afraid to <b>take risks</b> and/or <b>push the envelope</b> to give you something <b>new, fresh and cutting edge!</b><br><br>This <b>Mystery Project</b> is yet another testament to her <b>brilliance</b> as an author. Much like her other work, story is best dived into, <b>no blurb needed</b>. <i>But there will be a warning in blurb you should read!</i><br><br>This story offers <b>excellent character development, scorching sex scenes</b>, but above all a <b>plot</b> – a journey if you will – with <b>twists and turns</b> pushing the limits of <b>right and wrong</b> and exploring love, sexual attraction and <b>the hold it can have over you</b>. <br><br>I could not even put my Kindle down to go the bathroom that is how engulfed I was. Needless to say at 80% I was left hanging, but based on what I have read – this a <b>5-star story!</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>Be sure to <b>join Shh… [Smut, Heroes &amp; HEAs…] with Alessandra</b> here on GR for the latest news:<br><b><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/143204-shh-smut-heroes-heas-with-alessandra">https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/...</a></b><br><i>(Public group for members 18 years and older)</i><br><br><br><b><i>Alpha copy provided to me by author Alessandra Torre, in exchange for honest feedback &amp; review.</i><br><br><br>Thanks Alessandra! xo</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1003018463?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1003018463" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15890309138748580312"><b>More than 5 stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/2041ffa6-5bb0-49d9-8772-6065fb7f7b0e_zpsc1653185.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408958418i/10915280.jpg' alt=' photo 2041ffa6-5bb0-49d9-8772-6065fb7f7b0e_zpsc1653185.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I read a lot, and a lot of books I read stick with me, make me think, and stay on my mind. I’m not sure I’ve ever read a book thats hit me so hard and stuck with me as long as this. Days later and I can’t stop thinking about it! <br/><br/><i>Black Lies</i> is one of the most powerful, raw and all consuming love stories I have ever read. Was it selfish? Selfless? Maybe both. This love story was different than anything I’ve ever read before. It’s a story I’m sure I’ll never forget. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/b756dcf8-f5f5-490b-b5e8-4ae43eb56a39_zpsf0f97bb8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408857764i/10905996.jpg' alt=' photo b756dcf8-f5f5-490b-b5e8-4ae43eb56a39_zpsf0f97bb8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Meet <b>L</b></span>
  <span id="freeText15890309138748580312" style="display:none"><b>More than 5 stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/2041ffa6-5bb0-49d9-8772-6065fb7f7b0e_zpsc1653185.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408958418i/10915280.jpg" alt=" photo 2041ffa6-5bb0-49d9-8772-6065fb7f7b0e_zpsc1653185.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I read a lot, and a lot of books I read stick with me, make me think, and stay on my mind. I’m not sure I’ve ever read a book thats hit me so hard and stuck with me as long as this. Days later and I can’t stop thinking about it! <br><br><i>Black Lies</i> is one of the most powerful, raw and all consuming love stories I have ever read. Was it selfish? Selfless? Maybe both. This love story was different than anything I’ve ever read before. It’s a story I’m sure I’ll never forget. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/b756dcf8-f5f5-490b-b5e8-4ae43eb56a39_zpsf0f97bb8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408857764i/10905996.jpg" alt=" photo b756dcf8-f5f5-490b-b5e8-4ae43eb56a39_zpsf0f97bb8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Meet <b>Lana.</b> She’s a rich girl with rich parents who’s always wanted to do things her own way. She didn’t want to settle for what her parents wanted for her life. You will love her. You will hate her. You will despise some of the things she does. It was unfathomable to me. Then you will feel compassion. Heartbreak. Longing. Love. SHE will make you feel all those things. Then there is her man… Brant. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/43377066-85e1-4fda-8d70-dd6b4f73ac47_zpsed073e8a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408958418i/10915281.jpg" alt=" photo 43377066-85e1-4fda-8d70-dd6b4f73ac47_zpsed073e8a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Brant. </b>Brant is the man Lana’s been with for 3 years. The guy she’s in love with. He’s a rich genius. He loves Lana fiercely. He wants her to be his wife, to be his everything but she refuses to marry him. I loved Brant the entire book. I can’t think of a moment I didn’t. Which is why I had so much trouble with the concept of him. Of Lee. <br><br><b>Lee.</b> Lee is the guy Lana’s been seeing for 2 years. She did whatever she had to do to get him and she won’t give him up. He’s rough around the edges, he’s a landscaper and a ladies man. Lana wants him all to herself. There is something different about her relationship with Lee, but it’s clear that she loves him. And she loves Brant. She loves them both. <br><br>I know there are going to be some readers that are like… yeah, I figured this one out early and I say good for you. Me? It took me a long while. I’m talking close to 70% before I finally knew the big secret. Once you find out the twist in the story, it’s like a lightbulb goes off. Everything clicks into place. I don’t know how she does it, but every single detail lines up just the way its supposed to.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/062da794-33c4-4113-9b7c-f28eb6ea0012_zps616f7e60.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408958418i/10915282.jpg" alt=" photo 062da794-33c4-4113-9b7c-f28eb6ea0012_zps616f7e60.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I love an unpredictable story. The second I figured out what was going on, I called a friend who had read and talked it out, then I cried, then I finished the book, then I cried some more. <i>Black Lies</i> had such a profound effect on me, I even cried while making my images, just reading over the quotes. <br><i>
  <blockquote>True love makes a person reckless, makes them take risks and make sacrifices. True love tests the boundaries of our person, makes us yearn to be better and fight for the ground we stand on. I will fight for this love. Lie for it. Steal for it. It’s worthy of that. </blockquote>
</i> <br><br><i>
  <b>Black Lies</b>
</i> is a story of lies, secrets and betrayals, of unwavering love, loyalty and selflessness. A complete contradiction- but once you read, you’ll get it. As much as it may not seem like it, it’s an beautiful and intense love story above all else. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/ffa0cb16-0f98-43ea-999f-5945d3edbd31_zps3a9cad3c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408958418i/10915283.jpg" alt=" photo ffa0cb16-0f98-43ea-999f-5945d3edbd31_zps3a9cad3c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The more I’ve thought about it, I just know that this is going to be the best book I read this year. I can’t imagine anything topping it. It was that good. The concept was genius, the delivery was epic and the author is just brilliant! I am in awe! I don't even want to read other books right now... I just want to re-start this one and catch all the little things I know I missed. This is a book you need to one click the second it goes live. Go in blind and be prepared to be blown away! <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> She is more than my broken self will ever deserve, but I can never let her go, she owns, whether she knows it or not, all parts of me, every once of my body and soul. Her unconditional love brought me to life. Pulled me from a dry, lonely existence before saving me, quite literally, from myself.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/f8215fd9-0e8b-4165-831b-521eb480df5f_zpsb5a32fb8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408958418i/10915284.jpg" alt=" photo f8215fd9-0e8b-4165-831b-521eb480df5f_zpsb5a32fb8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/fbfe5257-5c23-4da3-b325-31eaf8f2110a_zpsd0802295.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399922023i/9610271.jpg" alt=" photo fbfe5257-5c23-4da3-b325-31eaf8f2110a_zpsd0802295.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15890309138748580312" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1038190367" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1038190367" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1038190367?book_show_action=true">Aug 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=6-star-books">6-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1038190367" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8436640898572406785"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 5+ STARS!!! :::</b><br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409256511i/10955241.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/665526.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>WOW WOW <em><strong>WOW</strong></em>!!! </b><br/><br/><em>Black Lies </em>was absolutely <em>brilliant!!! </em> A captivating, intriguing, and mysterious love story with a twist. It was addictive, enthralling, and incredibly well-written. This is one of those books that makes me want to go up to everyone and be like <b> YOU HAVE TO READ THIS NOW!!! </b><br/><br/>This is one of the most <em>complete</em> love stories I've ever read. It's a standalone with a fully resolved, and heart-warming ending but with the way the story unfolds</span>
  <span id="freeText8436640898572406785" style="display:none"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 5+ STARS!!! :::</b><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409256511i/10955241.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/665526.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>WOW WOW <em><strong>WOW</strong></em>!!! </b><br><br><em>Black Lies </em>was absolutely <em>brilliant!!! </em> A captivating, intriguing, and mysterious love story with a twist. It was addictive, enthralling, and incredibly well-written. This is one of those books that makes me want to go up to everyone and be like <b> YOU HAVE TO READ THIS NOW!!! </b><br><br>This is one of the most <em>complete</em> love stories I've ever read. It's a standalone with a fully resolved, and heart-warming ending but with the way the story unfolds, you realize just <em>how</em> deep their love truly is.<br><br>I know that some of you (like me) are going to be both intrigued but also scared by the blurb but please just <u>TRUST ME</u>. You all know the kinds of things that usually bother me and I promise you're safe to read this!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Brant: Became a tech billionaire by his twentieth birthday. Has been in a relationship with me for 3 years. Has proposed 4 times. Been rejected 4 times.<br><br>Lee: Cuts grass when he’s not banging housewives. Good with his hands, his mouth, and his cock. Has been pursued relentlessly by me for almost 2 years, whether he knows it or not.<br><br>Go ahead. Judge me. You have no idea what my love entails. If you think you’ve heard this story before, trust me – you haven’t.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>That last line is <em>especially</em> important. There is <em>so much more</em> to this love story beneath the surface.<br><br>What makes this story different than it seems? There is a twist. A secret that changes the whole dynamic of the story and it is <em>brilliantly</em> set up. Looking back, you'll see each of the hidden clues, all the layers of this secret, and it's so clever the way the author tells you exactly what is happening without ever saying it!<br><br>Whether you guess the twist early, or if you know about it before you start reading, or even find yourself completely surprised by it, won't make a difference. I think this is one of those stories you can enjoy no matter how you approach it because this journey is just as enthralling as the outcome.<br><br>In order to keep things spoiler-free, I'm going to tell you as little as possible about these characters because most anything I say (even names) is technically a spoiler. My only comment will be that I found it <em>so</em> refreshing to have such a <em>smart</em> heroine!! Please, when you're reading, don't judge her too quickly or harshly. I can honestly say that she's one of my favorite heroines. This is going to sound odd if you don't know the story but I absolutely <em>loved</em> the way she handled the situation she was put in. LOVED it!!!<br><br>I love stories where the lines are sometimes blurred but the love is unquestionable. You think you know whats happening but then you take a look from another angle and realize that nothing is as it seems. I know the blurb might sound scary to some of you but I promise you that there is <em>nothing</em> stupid or frustrating about any characters' actions. Once you see the complete picture, everything will all make sense.<br><br><em>Black Lies</em> is about people willing to go to any lengths to fight for their love and protect their relationship. My heart was racing as I read. My chest got tight the closer things got to coming out into the light. The layers of secrets and love are woven seamlessly together to create a rich, multi-layered story.<br><br>Ok... now, I'm going to be honest. I knew the twist before I started reading the book. I'm not a very trusting reader and with a story set up like this, I just <em>had</em> to know that this was actually a story I'd be okay with. So I found out first. But let me tell you, the moment I found out the twist, I literally dropped everything to start reading immediately. Personally, I felt like knowing in advance made me appreciate the story even more because I knew what to look for and I was able to enjoy the journey rather than worry about the outcome.<br><br>For me, the point was not being surprised by the twist, for me it was enjoying the story <em>with</em> the twist as a part of my understanding. I know that I personally loved the book as much as I did <i>because</i> I knew the twist. But every reader is different. I know that many of you love going into books blind and I fully respect that which is why I've kept this review spoiler free. But... for those of you who want to know about about cheating, love triangle, and HEA, click to read this hidden text: <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ok, so there’s technically no cheating. The two guys mentioned in the blurb are the same person — multiple personalities… they don’t even know about each other. She falls in love with the main guy, Brant, but when she learns about Lee, he’s a whole other person with a whole other life, and she sets out to make him fall in love with her too. She loves this man and wants him completely, even with his condition.<br><br>Brant and Lee don’t know they’re the same person. She is in a long-term relationship with Brant but sleeps with Lee. <u>But</u> she is <i>only</i> sleeping with Lee because she knows for a fact that he’s the same physical person as Brant. She isn’t actually cheating on Brant. In her eyes, she’s just falling for another side of his personality. She’s in love with both sides of him. <i>She just has to make both sides of him fall in love with her.</i><br><br>And yes, there's a HEA :) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Honestly guys, the <em>way</em> these characters loved each other was absolutely breathtaking. Unconventional to be sure, but all consuming and truly beautiful. I felt like I was left with the strong message that if you never stop believing in it, love will always find a way and it will last forever.<br><br>I can't recommend this book highly enough!! It's one of my new top favorites!!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I risked losing him. <br>I risked destroying his life. <br>I risked saving our love. <br>Our future."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><p>
  <strong>Rating: 5+ STARS!! Standalone.<br> Contemporary Adult romance.</strong>
</p><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1017679610" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1017679610" />
    <a title="Shurrn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn"><img alt="Shurrn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410564134p2/22115857.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1017679610?book_show_action=true">Aug 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shurrn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shurrn" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-modern">romance-modern</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1017679610" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4208449195978055234"><b>Are you ready to hear what I’m about to tell you? Brace yourself…<br/>THIS IS THE BEST THING I'VE READ ALL YEAR.<br/>There’s not even a close second right now.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407900338ra/10777549.gif' width='650' height='200' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Let me start by saying that you’ll find zero spoilers in this review.</i><br/><br/>I'm rating this 6 of 5 Stars, and I'm starting to believe Alessandra Torre might be an alien, because surely no human can be this fucking talented.<br/><br/>Alessandra Torre is unique in many ways – she blends sex, suspense, and romance in a way that keeps you on the edge of your seat. She i</span>
  <span id="freeText4208449195978055234" style="display:none"><b>Are you ready to hear what I’m about to tell you? Brace yourself…<br>THIS IS THE BEST THING I'VE READ ALL YEAR.<br>There’s not even a close second right now.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407900338ra/10777549.gif" width="650" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Let me start by saying that you’ll find zero spoilers in this review.</i><br><br>I'm rating this 6 of 5 Stars, and I'm starting to believe Alessandra Torre might be an alien, because surely no human can be this fucking talented.<br><br>Alessandra Torre is unique in many ways – she blends sex, suspense, and romance in a way that keeps you on the edge of your seat. She is one of a handful of my ‘stop-drop-and-read’ authors who ALWAYS deliver high-quality books which leave me with massive book-hangovers. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22471294.Black_Lies" title="Black Lies by Alessandra Torre" rel="nofollow noopener">Black Lies</a> was obviously no exception.<br><br><b>I am incapable of putting her books down.</b><br><br>They grab you from the opening lines and don’t let up. My responsibilities will be put off, husband will be ignored, my house could be on fire, Jake Bass could walk naked into my bedroom… Well… Ok, so I’d probably ask him to sit quietly on my bed until I was finished with the book... But you get the idea!<br><br>I have learned how I need to read her books: Block off several hours because the book WILL be finished in one sitting.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408289985ra/10832314.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here’s the thing about books that have “The Big Twist” – Sometimes you see it coming from a mile away, which is infuriating and makes the main character(s) look like idiots for not figuring it out too… Never the case with Torre. I was shocked… There’s no other way to describe it.<br><br>Alessandra Torre dangles the twist in front of your face from the opening pages… This “Secret” that keeps Brant from being the perfect man… This mysterious yet monumental character flaw which leads Layana to obsess over Lee despite the fact that she’s madly in love with Brant…<br><br>It was so easy to become enamored with this glorious romance…<br><i>Intelligent &amp; Intriguing Characters,<br>Amazing Dialogue,<br>Panty-Melting Sex,<br>…and all the while this unseen destructive force is lurking in the background.</i><br><br>Here’s the other thing about books that have “The Big Twist” – Sometimes the twist the only good thing about the book… Or worse, it makes the rest of the book bland in comparison – Ever go back by yourself and re-watch The Sixth Sense after you found out that Bruce Willis was dead the whole time? No? Can you remember anything else about that film other than this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408289985ra/10832315.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anything at all? Nope. Me neither… But then again, I review books, not movies ;)<br><br>…Once again, this was not the case with Black Lies. While I was monumentally shocked by Brant’s Secret, I was glued to this book from beginning to end – more on that in a moment - The reveal made me reflect on everything which preceded it. It made me understand Layana’s motives with a clarity I couldn’t grasp before… And I was desperate to find out what would happen next!<br><br><b>This is a love story which will leave you completely breathless.<br><br>Absolute Mind Blowing Perfection.<br>Go read this. Right this second.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408289985ra/10832316.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Let me tell you a bit about my experience reading this book…</b><br><br>I got an email at 4:42pm with an ARC attached. Ten minutes later Black Lies was on my Kindle tempting me with the book-version of bedroom eyes. <i>“Shurrn, read me!”</i> and I was all <i>“No, book! I have a review to write, and emails to return (sorry Rob), and laundry to do.”</i> But truthfully, I was already undressing it with my eyes…<br>Peeling back the cover…<br>Peaking at the first page…<br><br>I’m weak…<br><br>By 5:15pm I had walked my dogs, grabbed my iPhone, iPad, an iced coffee, and retreated to my bedroom – this is not an odd occurrence in my house. My darling husband is quite used to me “going into seclusion” when I have an awesome book in my hands… He also had the pleasure of seeing me read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18627715.Sex_Love_Repeat" title="Sex Love Repeat by Alessandra Torre" rel="nofollow noopener">Sex Love Repeat</a> last year while rocking back and forth on the couch like a deranged person… So yeah… I hide my insanity in the bedroom now… Fewer witnesses.<br><br>I spent the rest of the evening completely sucked into this book – eyes wide, pages turning frantically, my mind desperately trying to figure out what “The Secret” could possibly be…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408289985ra/10832317.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At 7:10pm I finally hit the twist.<br>I yelled.<br>It was loud.<br>Through the closed door my husband hears me scream <i>
  <b>“OH MY FUCKING GOD!”</b>
</i> but he was unfazed. As I mentioned earlier, he has prior knowledge of my love of (and reactions to) Alessandra Torre…<br><br>I couldn’t sit down and read any longer.<br>I had to pace around the room clutching my iPad with a white-knuckled grip…<br><br>By 11:00pm I was completely finished. Emotionally exhausted. Social Media outlets were informed… And I was sitting in my bed trying to convince myself not to flip to the first page and read the entire thing again… Real Life (the one I had ignored all evening) was going to intrude on my post-book-reading bliss early the following morning.<br><br>I dreamed about this book.<br><br><b>I woke up the next morning and started re-reading Black Lies while brushing my teeth.</b><br><br>Did I mention that I’m weak?<br><br>It was even better the second time around… <br>I got to pick up on the mountain of clues and breadcrumbs scattered throughout the text like glittering jewels…<br><br>Nearly 48 hours after finishing this book (The second time) it was still stuck in my head – I was having a drink with a friend, gushing all over my enjoyment of this book when she said, <i>“Sounds like you’ve got a major hard on for another piece of Fiction…”</i><br><br>My response, straight faced:<br><b>“If this book had a dick, I would get down on my knees and suck it.”</b><br><br>So there you have it. I can’t think of a better way to tell you how awesome this book is…<br><br>Read it.<br>When you discover Brant’s secret for yourself, message me. I’ll be there to help you recover.<br><br><b>Alessandra Torre,</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408289985ra/10832318.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404328860ra/10226023.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>***Alessandra Torre graciously provided me with an ARC of this book in exchange for an honest review***</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4208449195978055234" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

They were divided on this book so I'm going to read something else by her before my final determination.<br>But this one?<br><a href="http://imgur.com/Jdl4RAX" rel="nofollow noopener">

She pissed me off.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/OyfOyg4" rel="nofollow noopener">

The love affair that is boring as crap.<br>Then she meets Lee. Does him too. <br>(it's not cheating-so don't get your panties in a wad)<br>She connives her way into his life and runs off his girlfriend. Then she lets him talk to her like a dog. Calls her the slut. WTF?<br> <br>I don't like any of these damn characters. <br><br>Then the BIG TWIST!!!<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Fuck me sideways, he has multiple personalities that his weirdo aunt is exploiting to make them even more money. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>My answer to this whole book is:<br><a href="http://imgur.com/mciVuLV" rel="nofollow noopener">

It gave me a special, second, emotionally intense experience. <b>Obsessed with this emotive story.</b> I'll read this story again and </span>
  <span id="freeText16955779200657382420" style="display:none">**SPOILER FREE review**<br>* <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Black-Lies-Alessandra-Torre-ebook/dp/B00N0EQM6Y/ref=pd_rhf_se_p_dnr_2" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> * <a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Black-Lies-Alessandra-Torre-ebook/dp/B00N0EQM6Y/ref=sr_1_2?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1408955473&amp;sr=8-2&amp;keywords=black+lies" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a> *<br><br><b>6 Million Sexy <i>Mind Fucking</i> Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407833548i/10770024.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>This story is a suspenseful slice of wonderful.</b> <br><br>Alessandra Torre is the Queen of erotic story telling with an addictive, intriguing quality. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408094180i/10805980.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The balance of words is<i> exquisite.</i></b><br><br>The first time, I devoured this story in 24 hours, the next; I slowly read and absorbed every nuance and inflection. It gave me a special, second, emotionally intense experience. <b>Obsessed with this emotive story.</b> I'll read this story again and again and I'll love these characters forever,<i> all of them.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407776831i/10764128.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Be prepared to have your mind played with, tugged this way and that. I went through the<i> crazy-feels</i>, all sorts of emotions and possibilities swirling round my head,<i> I absolutely loved the experience. </i>It made me feel, it made me think, it made me question <i>why?</i> And it made me cry. Ultimately the powerful writing captivated me, caught me in its net of<b> Black Lies</b> and I could not put it down. I had to devour <b> this story as quickly as my life would allow.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408098460i/10806241.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I won’t say too much about the story for fear of spoiling your experience. I can only provide snippets of the characters, and my <i> feelings, emotions, and lovely thoughts; </i>tell you about the truly genius writing that makes <b>Black Lies</b> so incredibly good. <br><br>Allow the story to completely unravel; feel your way through. <b>Reserve your judgement and keep your mind open.</b> This book is so worth the patience, understanding and crazy mind fuck of a ride it takes you on.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408354535i/10840354.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We glimpse into the kind of life the characters have lived, privileged, tricky and skewed in places…. <br><br><b>“Brant Sharp. Genius. Billionaire. Philanthropist.” </b> Sexy and intense.<b> “Quietly confident. Unassuming. Gorgeous.” </b> He's completely dreamy and utters the most beautiful words to Lana. <br><br>Heiress, <b>Layana (Lana) Fairmont,</b> is a girl who wants an ordinary life and, what she wants is just about within her reach..... I was completely won over by her honest words and thoughts. Honesty can be hard to take. She may have done things that made me gasp but by that point I was hers; she was my friend. A heroine with courage, love, sass, and complete sexual awareness. <br><br>Lee… <b>“Cocky. Confident. Sexual.”</b><i> I love him and his HOTNESS.</i> He excited me. I loved every aspect of his personality. <br><br><b>How to choose between them? </b><br><br>I felt torn as a reader….. Found love for<b> all 3 characters. </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408094260i/10805982.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Readers you will NOT have heard anything like this story before. It’s a <b>masterpiece</b> of<b> erotic </b>writing that has the <b>unique stamp of Alessandra Torre</b> all over it. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408707296i/10884787.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Every reader needs to experience the secrets and lies, <i>feel the angst.</i> I went through a range of emotions and thoughts.<br><br><b>I felt the intense passion and sexual quality.</b><br><br><b> Black Lies </b>is a beautiful love story with a mind fuck of originality and suspense twisting its way through. There are lies, secrets, despicable goings on, but at the heart of this story I truly experienced love, soul defining, deep, powerful love. And, of course, the <b>sex is absolutely stunning in every way. </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422998574i/13574389.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Dirty, delicious, wild sex. </b><br><br>It twisted my mind, played with my book soul and captured my heart. I felt an impending something but, what I didn’t know? Peel away the layers as you read…. Enjoy the subtle nuances and edge of your seat addictive quality, wrapped in a cocoon of sexy eroticism. It kept my heart thumping; it gave me butterflies, sexy excitement and nervous, angsty anticipation. <i> It’s incredible.</i> <b>Perfect. Dramatic. Timing. I seriously couldn’t put it down.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408099004i/10806323.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Black Lies, in true Alessandra Torre style, tells the story from the point of view of various characters, which, for me, completely enhances the dramatic quality and tension. The writing is stylish and unique, and flows around your mind with ease. It emotes feelings and creates thoughts at the perfect moments. There were times I felt my heart squeeze at the underlying sadness, and times I felt incredulous despair at the heroine. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408354581i/10840355.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I read, I don’t want to notice I’m reading, I want to feel completely immersed in a world that’s as real as the breath that I breathe. I want to not just see pictures but feel them; feel the passion, the angst, the craziness, I want to have questions and be able to seek answers, I want an EPIC read and that's what Alessandra Torre gives me as an author. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422997794i/13574285.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Trust</b> in the storytelling.<b> Trust</b> you'll be taken on a wild reading adventure go with the flow of this book… I smiled, I cried, I went a little crazy. <i>Needed someone to hold my hand.</i> <b>I adored.</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408995892i/10919052._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Alessandra Torre sprinkled her QUEEN of storytelling magic all over this beauty. <i>If I could wipe my mind and read it all over again I would!</i></b><br><br>A reading experience I won't forget. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408354712i/10840361.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><u>To help the reader ‘feels’ of this story.</u><br><b>The heroine may do things you loath…. You will question her actions. She may become intolerable to you. Love or hate her, just keep reading, you’ll be so close to the spectacular climax of the story. The truth is out there. It’s hidden deep, and it’s beautiful. </b><br><br><br>A <b>standalone</b> for all readers of romance, erotica and mind blowing stories that make your heart beat fast.<br><br>Draft copy generously given by the author for my honest thoughts ♥<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1553814205" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13814658111225539141"><b>A gazillion stars...</b> One of my all-times-favorites!<br/><br/>Is there anyone who still hasn't read this book? <br/>If so, you don't know what you are missing! <br/>Please do read this book. <br/><br/>This is <b>a spoiler-free review</b> which will mess with your mind as much as the book does! Go ahead and give it a chance! You won't regret, I promise...<br/><br/>But please... pretty please, read this book without knowing the plot twist. <b>DO NOT READ any spoilers</b> anywhere, which would definitely ruin the book for you. <br/><br/><b>The blurb and the reality</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13814658111225539141" style="display:none"><b>A gazillion stars...</b> One of my all-times-favorites!<br><br>Is there anyone who still hasn't read this book? <br>If so, you don't know what you are missing! <br>Please do read this book. <br><br>This is <b>a spoiler-free review</b> which will mess with your mind as much as the book does! Go ahead and give it a chance! You won't regret, I promise...<br><br>But please... pretty please, read this book without knowing the plot twist. <b>DO NOT READ any spoilers</b> anywhere, which would definitely ruin the book for you. <br><br><b>The blurb and the reality:</b><br><br>I must say that this book is nothing like you may assume after reading the blurb. This is an unbelievable journey, <b>a mind-blowing</b> reading experience. <br><br>The blurb might make you think that this is going to be a dirty book – a love affair of a woman with low moral values with two men that are the opposite of one another. Oh, the reality is far from it, believe me!<br><br><i><b>Brant:</b> <br>Became a tech billionaire by his twentieth birthday. <br>Has been in a relationship with Layana for 3 years.<br>Has proposed 4 times. Been rejected 4 times.<br><br><b>Lee:</b> <br>Cuts grass when he’s not banging housewives.<br> Good with his hands, his mouth, and his cock. <br>Has been pursued relentlessly by Layana for almost 2 years, whether he knows it or not.</i><br><br>Our heroine <b>Layana</b> says:<br> <i>Go ahead. Judge me. <br>You have no idea what my love entails. <br>I love two men. <br>I f*ck two men. <br>If you think you’ve heard this story before, you haven’t.</i><br><br><b>I hear you saying this:</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416466073ra/11971173.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Yes, you will be saying it a lot...</b><br><br>She will shock you, shake you, irritate you. <br>You will hate her, you will despise her, you will not understand her for a while. <br><br>And when you understand her...<br>You will love her, you will adore her, you will applaud her... <br>You will be sorry for her, you will ache for her...<br>You will desperately wish a HEA for her...<br><br><b>No I am not kidding... I am dead serious!</b><br><br>As soon as you start the book, in the prologue, you will read about how Layana stalked Lee (the second man in her life) and how she ended his relationship with another woman. <br><br>These are her words of victory: <br><br><i>“That’s right. Turn and walk your pretty self away from this man. He will no longer touch your face. He will no longer make love to your body. He is mine. I will take your place...<br>Victory is mine. I grinned, giving myself a virtual high five, and put my Mercedes into drive... Maybe after my massage I’d swing by my boyfriend’s office. Drop off a sandwich for him. Celebrate my victory with the other man in my life.” </i><br><br><b>Do you feel like this? I did :)</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460067970ra/18694288.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, Layana really stalks Lee, even hires a private detective, makes careful and evil plans and ends his relationship with his girlfriend Molly.<br><br><i>“Hello stalking, I am Layana. Pleased to make your acquaintance.”<br>“I sat and watched. Focused in and spied. Growled into a stale handful of nuts as I saw pieces of what might be love...<br>I needed a plan. I had seen enough. What I needed to figure out was how to destroy them.”<br>“Soon, everything would be fixed. Soon, Lee would be fully mine. Tomorrow would be a big day. A relationship-ending one.”</i><br><br><b>Now, how can you love this heroine? How can you feel anything positive for a woman who says this and does all these things? </b><br><br>Well, I loved her. I adored her. I felt sorry for her... <br>Hey, <b>DON’T JUDGE ME</b>, read it and adore her yourself...<br><br>After reading the blurb and the prologue, and some chapters, you will have some clear assumptions. Let me tell you that <b>YOU CAN’T BE MORE WRONG</b>.<br><br>This book will mess with your mind until you finally learn the facts. But the facts won’t come easily. There will be breadcrumbs in every chapter, one contradicting the other...<br><br><b>You will be like this - constantly:</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460067970ra/18694289.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>And like this:</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460067970ra/18694290.gif" width="425" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book will shock you in each chapter. Just as you think you have understood something, in the next chapter, you will see that you can’t be further from the truth.<br><br>The writer will play with you like a puppet and you will definitely enjoy the ride.<br><br>After finishing the book, if you go back and reread it, you will see that the writer has, in fact, been telling you exactly what is happening without actually saying it, but you are clueless while reading it, unfortunately :)<br><br>It just is so cleverly written that it is impossible not to admire the talent of the writer... That was really refreshing and nothing similar to I have read before.<br><br>Let me shock you a little bit more (This is a spoiler-free review - no worries:)<br><br>The title of the book is <b>BLACK LIES</b>.<br><br>Who tells black lies in this book? <br>Well – everybody does:<br><br><i>“True love makes a person reckless, makes them take risks and make sacrifices. True love tests the boundaries of our person, makes us yearn to be better and fight for the ground we stand on. I will fight for this love. Lie for it. Steal for it. It is worthy of that. This love is worth the unsaid truths. The hidden lies.”<br><br>“I might have gone years without discovering his secret. He certainly hid it well enough... I wasn’t the only clueless one.”<br><br>***<br><br>“It took nine months for me to discover the secret. It could have taken even longer. I look back now and see very little clues.”<br><br>***<br><br>“It was a wonderful story. Poetic in its portrayal of his life. Endearing. The creation of this tortured, confused man before me. Perfectly explained his desperation for love, mixed with a side of I’llNeverBeGoodEnough. Too bad it was all a lie. I laid in his arms and wondered how many women he had told it to.”<br><br>***<br><br>“God. I knew. So many things wrong with this picture. But God, it felt so good. I stared into his eyes, listened to him whisper my name, and enjoyed every second of the ride. For those minutes, I forgot about Brant, about Tennis Barbie, about anything but him and me and that moment of time. I was his rebound. He was my sidepiece. And both of us wanted more. At least I did. Maybe anything else was a lie I was telling myself.”<br><br>***<br><br>“Lies. Lies are keeping us apart. I started this relationship with one lie... She started this relationship clean and innocent, and has piled on the lies since then.”</i><br><br>In the end, you will understand why they have been telling lies all along...<br><br><b>How about cheating??? Read this and surprise yourself even more!</b><br><br><b>Brant: </b><br><i>“I just want to know why. Why does she cheat on me? What do I not provide for her? What part of me is not good enough? Why, when her love for me burns bright enough to singe… does she sneak off with a stranger? My biggest fear is that she loves him. My biggest fear is that he has wormed his way into her heart. I love her too much to share her. I hate him with a vengeance that turns my blood white.”</i><br><br><b>Lee:</b><br><i>“I love you too much to leave you. But I can’t do this. It is killing me.” <br>Then he said the words I dreaded, the ones I never wanted to hear but that had stalked me in my dreams. <br>“You have to choose. You have to.”<br><br>“Tell me what you want. If you want it, I’ll leave. <br>Not for him. I’ll never do anything for him. <br>But for you, I’ll do it. <br>I’ll fucking kill myself...”</i><br><br><b>Jillian</b> (Brant’s aunt) when she sees Layana with Lee:<br><i>“You selfish stupid girl.” She pointed a strong finger toward the bar. “He’ll leave you, Layana. One day, you’ll wake up, and that boy in there will be gone . Brant loves you. He’ll be with you forever.”</i><br><br><b>Layana:</b><br><i>“Yes, I am taking the biggest gamble of my life. I love them both too much to do anything else.”</i><br><br><b>Feeling like this?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460067970ra/18694291.gif" width="425" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>OK, now... Stop... Don’t judge! You will love them...</b><br>WTF ? :)))<br>Well, you think you have understood what this book is about now that you have read some quotations... right?<br>Sorry to tell you but you haven't!<br>Read and see what I mean! <br><br>Theirs was a wonderful love, so deep, so strong, so unique...<br>You are telling me <b>WTF again</b>? With all these lies and the cheating and the stalking and evil plans? <br><br><b>Yes, I am telling you exactly that.</b><br><br>You will only understand how deep and precious their love is when you read the book as the story unfolds itself...<br><br>OK, now... Feel more shocked, I am saying it: I am definitely, absolutely and completely <b>TEAM LAYANA</b>... <br>You can’t believe it, right. Go read it and you will be Team Layana, too...<br><br>Somewhere in the book, Layana tells us, the readers, this:<br><br><i>“I know you don’t understand. I know you hate me. But you will soon find out... And once you find out, you will understand. You would have done the same thing.”</i><br><br>And I am answering for myself: <br><b>I would have done the same thing!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460068856ra/18694350.gif" width="425" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Please... Drop everything and read this book.<br>I am sure at the end, you will be saying, <b>“Wow... Just wow...”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457041995ra/18312975.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Taking a plot like this is risky. <br>(And while saying “a plot like this”, I don’t mean “cheating” at all!!! Don't go and read a review where you will learn "what the plot is actually about". Please, make sure you yourself learn it while reading)<br>OK, I was saying that dealing with a plot like this is risky because if you fail with a plot like this, you fail big. But then, if you succeed with a plot like that, it is bound to be a masterpiece. <br><br>And this book is A MASTERPIECE, just brilliant ! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447249790ra/16976680.gif" width="430" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I hope <b>I have been able to mess with your mind enough</b> to intrigue you to drop everything and read this book :)<br><br>P.S. Please, read this book without knowing the plot twist, DO NOT READ any spoilers that would ruin the book for you.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13814658111225539141" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1036842334" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1036842334" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1036842334?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1036842334" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8920671101761515739"><b>1.5 stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=6gyn29' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409222920ra/10950394.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I'm definitely, definitely in the small minority when it comes to this book. A lot of my GR buddies loved this. So I would say that don't let my review discourage you from reading this book. Honestly, the twist was great. If you want some great mind-fuck, definitely read this book.<br/><br/>To be fair, I figured out the "BIG SECRET" fairly early on and I asked a couple of friends for confirmation and they told me I was right. So I wasn't really surprised and the clues were plenty. But I stil</span>
  <span id="freeText8920671101761515739" style="display:none"><b>1.5 stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=6gyn29" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409222920ra/10950394.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'm definitely, definitely in the small minority when it comes to this book. A lot of my GR buddies loved this. So I would say that don't let my review discourage you from reading this book. Honestly, the twist was great. If you want some great mind-fuck, definitely read this book.<br><br>To be fair, I figured out the "BIG SECRET" fairly early on and I asked a couple of friends for confirmation and they told me I was right. So I wasn't really surprised and the clues were plenty. But I still continued reading because a) I already bought the book and it seems idiotic to return it, and b) I was really curious about how the author was going to pull it off. I personally don't like this plot device in my romance books. In any other genre, I would have loved it. But in contemporary/erotic romance, (at least that is what this book is categorized in), I'm not crazy about it. For one, most authors take too much liberty in fictionalizing something that is very serious. To me that just invites criticism. Second, some authors write their beliefs into how to deal with said conditions even though it goes against what is accepted scientific knowledge, *cough* Katy Evans *cough* and that just makes me uncomfortable.<br><br>That said, I think this book tried. It really did. But it spent too much time in setting up the BIG SECRET and hiding the BIG SECRET that all the other aspects that could have made this a compelling read became secondary to the BIG SECRET. So it's really no surprise that I didn't enjoy it as much. <br><br>Speaking of compelling characters, what dragged the rating down for me was Layana. Aside from that Brant was just meh. Lee, same thing. Their characters were just...I don't know -- lifeless and one-dimensional to me. Layana's actions in particular just turned me off. Even after she wised up, she did too many unforgivable things in my eyes, and looking at it in the context of the BIG SECRET, there was no way I could ever be Team Layana after that. <br><br>Another thing I wasn't particularly fond of was how the BIG SECRET was handled (more on that later). There were too many inconsistencies to me. Small details like the year Apple II was released or which computer IBM released in 1997 drove me up the wall. I know, I know. It's nitpicking to the highest degree but I already know the secret so my brain started picking on those details. In my defense, these things affected the whole timeline of events, so I felt totally justified. Don't judge, mmkay?<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=29xejvn" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409222920ra/10950395.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Please don't click if you haven't read the book yet! Please! I am putting this in because I need to vent a little bit. So don't hate me.</b><br><br><i>**This is a very long rant/review so be warned.</i><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[So Layana...I'm sorry but I have a major bone to pick with this character. When she found out that Brandt has DID, what did she do? Oh she called Jillian. The one person she said she doesn't trust. I understand she would call her the first time but in two years TWO YEARS, it never occurred to her to Google and do research on her own about Brant's condition??? <br><br>At first, I thought, huh, maybe she doesn't really know a whole lot about it. But when she told Brant, it was like WTF!! This girl knew all along what his condition meant and she went and told him without the presence of a professional?? It was like she was just telling him something mundane, "Hey, babe. You have spinach stuck in your teeth. Oh, by the way, you're suffering from DID and the guy I'm fucking is actually one of your alters." <br><br>I mean, srsly? And this coming from someone who was constantly described throughout the books as being EXTREMELY INTELLIGENT!! LOL!! I swears, every time I read that my head just explodes. I just couldn't fathom why she never thought about calling in a second opinion in the whole two years she kept the BIG SECRET. This was completely out of character because I know she could totally make shit happen. <br><br>Case in point, the things she did to Lee -- again, I'm sorry but this is the part where I almost DNF the book. She knew about his DID. She knew who Lee was and yet she deliberately set out to manipulate his break up with Molly. I couldn't reconcile the fact that she was able to do that and yet she was unable to ask anyone about his condition! I just couldn't, okay? In this day and age, it's virtually impossible. And the ironic thing is, Brant's primary business is technology. Call me a nit-picky bitch but there is still such a thing as consistency. And no, I don't accept it's because of lurve. Lurve, my ass. <br><br>And another thing, do these people live in a vacuum??? Layana has no friends whatsoever. She only mentions "friends" and acquaintances (with disdain) in passing. She supposedly has an army of servants at her beck and call, and yet it was just that easy to keep everyone from guessing the whole SECRET. The fact that she's been in magazines, no one recognized her traipsing around with Lee/Brant? <br><br>And Brant, no one noticed him. Ever? The other side of town isn't convincing enough for me to believe that no one, not in this day age, and certainly not in over two decades, ever noticed him. It isn't like Brant doesn't appear in society. He wasn't a recluse. He definitely shows his face around. And yet no one recognized him as Lee. Jillian would have to pay more than half of San Francisco to keep it under wraps. I don't buy the whole "shadow" thing. It's a logistical nightmare. The fact that she had done it for over three decades plus was just unbelievable. I'm sorry but I could not suspend my disbelief over that. <br><br>Also, Jillian said that there were other personalities aside from Lee, how or why these personalities come out wasn't explained at all. And this is why I hate the mental illness/DID trope being used in romance. To me, at least, you'd have to at least give a factual narrative about DID. DID is already a very controversial topic. The scientific community is still pretty much divided about it. No court would even accept DID as a defense or as a plea and yet Jillian was able to get a judge to sign over Brant's rights to her. I know. Crooked judge and doctor AKA convenient plot device. But I digress. <br><br>I know AT had taken liberties with it. I understand why she had to do that. Unfortunately, it was the kind of liberties that made me uncomfortable. The fact that it was made as though these personalities come out on a whim was just stretching it. And stress alone isn't reason enough to make these personalities come out. It has to be a specific stressor related to the trauma that brought about the personality break in the first place. I won't bore you with the details but I just can't deal with those liberties being taken. Especially when the main character, a character who supposedly loved this person, blatantly put this man's psyche in a very dangerous position. It was just idiotic when Layana was thinking how many more personalities she could coax out and play. Good Gawd! Her reason for doing it was laughable. It wasn't because of love. It was all about ownership. She wants all of him and doesn't like to share. Well, boo-hoo. <br><br>The whole trauma thing was just unconvincing to me as well. First of all, scientifically, nothing is set in stone yet. I'm not saying what happened to Brant and what he witnessed wasn't horrible but it was just all very convenient especially the way he suddenly remembers everything. Considering that he seems to have a normal childhood prior to that trauma, the whole outcome was a little improbable. <br><br>I wasn't too crazy about Jillian or his parents either. Same thing. After all these years, his parents didn't question Jillian at all. They unequivocally trusted her? That's just so farfetched. They'd have to be deaf, blind and mute not to notice. And Brant. For someone so highly intelligent, he didn't even care to find out if what Jillian was feeding him was bullshit. It would have worked if he's 12 but he's 38-freakin'-years old. And he's intelligent! He has resources. <br><br>And not one character in this book acted sane. Holy freakin' hell. All of them, from his parents, Layana, Jillian needs to be in therapy. Seriously. It seemed to me like this book was one whole convenient plot device and all to conceal the BIG SECRET. To me, it lacked real conflict. I don't consider Layana's manipulations as conflict at all. <br><br>Maybe I would have felt more if Lee was given a POV. I don't know. That seems like a great red herring to throw out there. But we didn't get it so we'll never know.<br><br>The epilogue was good but I'm wondering why Jillian was the only one there. Truthfully, Layana deserves to be imprisoned too. The way she refers to Brant as her property was just sickening especially in the context of his DID. Why isn't Layana in that cell with Jillian? She should have been in my opinion. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Sorry for the rant but I just need to get it off my chest. So there.<br><br>In other words, this book relied too much on one massive plot twist, which I already had issues with. It got better for me towards the end when the characters started using their brain. But by the time, these characters acted sane enough to call a professional, I was done. I just couldn't find any more fucks to give. So 1.5 stars. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8920671101761515739" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1015468013" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16939251201498925430"><b> 5 Iwannafuckyourighthere Stars </b><br/><br/><a href='https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/14830069852' title='Screenshot_1 by Book Worm, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407185148i/10652346.jpg' width='400' height='519' alt='Screenshot_1' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I’m not going to tell you what this book is about. What I am going to tell you is simple. <b> Go in blind, go in with an open mind. </b> Hidden secrets lurk throughout this book, throughout her story and their journey – these are secrets that you must discover for yourself. Truths that need to be pulled from the lies by your own hands.<br/><br/>Alessandra Torre, this woman’s talent shined in this book. Having experienced all of her prior books, I can honestly say she outdid he</span>
  <span id="freeText16939251201498925430" style="display:none"><b> 5 Iwannafuckyourighthere Stars </b><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/14830069852" title="Screenshot_1 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407185148i/10652346.jpg" width="400" height="519" alt="Screenshot_1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’m not going to tell you what this book is about. What I am going to tell you is simple. <b> Go in blind, go in with an open mind. </b> Hidden secrets lurk throughout this book, throughout her story and their journey – these are secrets that you must discover for yourself. Truths that need to be pulled from the lies by your own hands.<br><br>Alessandra Torre, this woman’s talent shined in this book. Having experienced all of her prior books, I can honestly say she outdid herself with Black Lies. This is not a simple tale of love and deceit. This is a story about loving so fiercely that you push beyond your own comfort. <b>Sacrifice everything. Risking it all to save everything. </b><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/14827359381" title="Screenshot_2 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407185148i/10652347._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="593" alt="Screenshot_2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I went into self-preservation mode the moment I opened this book. From the first words, <i>my heart rate spiked, knots pulled taut and the butterflies swirled. </i> No matter what walls I built, Alessandra shattered them. Not piece by piece, <i>but with a sledgehammer</i> – one moment I was on the outside looking in and then suddenly I was submerged. <br><br>There is not a box that this story can fit into. It will stretch you, bend you to the point where you think you’ll break, it will turn you on and it will turn you inside out. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/14830069782" title="Screenshot_3 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407185148i/10652348.jpg" width="400" height="267" alt="Screenshot_3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/14643803848" title="Screenshot_4 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407185148i/10652349._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="548" alt="Screenshot_4" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>True love makes a person reckless, makes them take risks and make sacrifices. True love tests the boundaries of our person, makes us yearn to be better and fight for the ground we stand on. I will fight for this love. Love for it. Steal for it. </b>
</i> <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/14830435515" title="Screenshot_5 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407185148i/10652350.jpg" width="400" height="525" alt="Screenshot_5" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I will leave you with this advice. <b>Read it. </b> Hold your judgments, open your heart &amp; your mind and let Alessandra lead you into this messy love story. <u> I promise you</u>, when you turn that final page you will not regret it.<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/14643778739" title="Screenshot_6 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407185148i/10652351.jpg" width="400" height="327" alt="Screenshot_6" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/14830069722" title="Screenshot_7 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407185148i/10652352._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="602" alt="Screenshot_7" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i> Advanced kindly provided by the author. <br></i></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>
