        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1002644311" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1647433176869904303"><b>
  <i>Spoiler FREE review posted 8.25.14</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>4 Unlike Anything You've Read Before Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408658716i/10880214._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <br/>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>I love her completely. She returns the love wildly. This love is worth the unsaid truths. The hidden lies.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408658716ra/10880215.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Do you hate love triangles?</b><br/>Read. This. Book.<br/><b>Do you dislike cheating?</b><br/>Read. This. Book.<br/><b>Do you want an unputdownable, erotic story filled with so many twists and turns your head will spin and keep you up all night till you're finished?</b><br/>READ. THIS. BOOK.<br/><br/>Bravo, Ms. Torre, for writing a story unlike any I</span>
  <span id="freeText1647433176869904303" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Spoiler FREE review posted 8.25.14</i>
</b><br><br><b>4 Unlike Anything You've Read Before Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408658716i/10880214._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I love her completely. She returns the love wildly. This love is worth the unsaid truths. The hidden lies.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408658716ra/10880215.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Do you hate love triangles?</b><br>Read. This. Book.<br><b>Do you dislike cheating?</b><br>Read. This. Book.<br><b>Do you want an unputdownable, erotic story filled with so many twists and turns your head will spin and keep you up all night till you're finished?</b><br>READ. THIS. BOOK.<br><br>Bravo, Ms. Torre, for writing a story unlike any I've ever read before. I can tell you that this is not a book I will be soon forgetting. All I can tell you is that you <b>MUST</b> go into this blind. Do not read any reviews, stay away from any and all spoilers. Just read it. If you've read the blurb, that's <b>ALL</b> you need to know. Trust me on this. Any minor details can be a huge spoiler. So my review will not give you any of the meat of the story. I'll simply graze the surface<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408658716ra/10880216.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Layana</b><br>Or Lana for short (which let me tell you, I gots a little thrill out of. Since I finally have a book where the heroine does my name justice.) But I digress...<br>In typical A. Torre fashion, she writes a heroine that's confident, has her faults but owns them, and owns her sexuality without a blush in sight.<br><br>You'll love her at times, hate her at others, feel for her, cry with her, and love with her. That's no small feat to accomplish, let me tell you.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408658716i/10880218._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Brant: <br><i>Became a tech billionaire by his twentieth birthday. Has been in a relationship with me for 3 years.<br>Has proposed 4 times. Been rejected 4 times.</i></b><br><br>Brandt is a character that is difficult not to fall in love with right away. His connection with Layana is instant, but the relationship builds throughout the books as it progresses through over 2 years.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408658716i/10880219._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lee:<br>Cuts grass when he’s not banging housewives. Good with his hands, his mouth, and his cock. Has been pursued relentlessly by me for almost 2 years, whether he knows it or not.</b><br><br>And that's all you get. Nothing more.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408658716ra/10880220.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The sex</b><br>Hot. As. Fuck. If you've never read a book by this author, start with this one. You'll be hooked. I guarantee you.<br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I thought you were a man of action. You nervous? Worried you can't compete?<br>"I'm worried I'll fuck you so well I'll ruin you for life."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408658716ra/10880221.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The love scenes were erotic but at the same time filled with emotion. Whether that was lust, love, anger, fear, it was always there. And it made it that much better.<br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">He fucked me to use me, his focus on his pleasure, his attraction to me not masked it any way. It should have felt wrong, it shouldn't have been hot, but it was, dirty and desperate, and I came hard, my hands gripping the rough brick, my legs shaking, the pleasure ripping a forbidden path through my body.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>So why only 4 stars? Well, I figured out the big "secret" fairly early in. Around 35% to be precise. That made the reveal towards the end a bit anticlimactic for me. But fortunately, that wasn't all there was to it. There was so much more wrapped up and around this secret and revealed. The author drops some big hints while at the same time trickle feeding you the information chapter by chapter. One thing I can tell you, whether you figure out the secret early or not, you WILL be up reading until you get to the last page. This book was unputdownable for me. I read it in practically one sitting. And of course, leave it to A. Torre to go out with a bang with that last chapter. The perfect conclusion to one mind fuck of a book.<br><br>My recommendation? READ IT. It's just one of those books you need to experience.<br><br><b>
  <i>If you think you’ve heard this story before, trust me – you haven’t</i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408658716ra/10880222.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And that's no lie.<br><br><i>ARC courtesy of author in exchange for an honest review</i></span>

<div id="review_968719164" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/968719164" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/968719164?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=alpha-heroes">alpha-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=choke-dat-ho">choke-dat-ho</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=panty-dropping-hot">panty-dropping-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=netgalley-edelweiss">netgalley-edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=what-are-you-trying-to-say">what-are-you-trying-to-say</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer968719164" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14662198314200417053"><b>2.5 stars!</b><br/><br/><i>I originally rated this 3.5 stars and after letting the shock wear off for a day or two, chatted with a good friend and we both thought the author didn't do her research well in regards to the "twist." If you want a more comprehensive and in-depth look to the numerous plot holes we discussed, check out my friend's review <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1036842334?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a>. This is why I'm changing my rating to 2.5 stars.</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409071760i/10929847._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I’ve only read one other Alessandra Torre book but I can already tell she does not deliver stories that follow a </span>
  <span id="freeText14662198314200417053" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars!</b><br><br><i>I originally rated this 3.5 stars and after letting the shock wear off for a day or two, chatted with a good friend and we both thought the author didn't do her research well in regards to the "twist." If you want a more comprehensive and in-depth look to the numerous plot holes we discussed, check out my friend's review <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1036842334?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a>. This is why I'm changing my rating to 2.5 stars.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409071760i/10929847._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’ve only read one other Alessandra Torre book but I can already tell she does not deliver stories that follow a straight line. I like this unpredictability factor, and her writing is amazing – once I started the book I didn’t stop until I was finished. I can totally see why this book would be a 5 star/6 star favorite for many; heck, I was pretty sure it’d be a 5 star winner for me as well. The lies, the intricately-woven mystery and the addictive writing all hinted at a flawless read for me. Unfortunately, there were several issues I had with it and as much I liked the concept of the book, the execution of the original premise fell flat. I have to stress here that I <i>did</i> like it. I just didn’t love it. <br><br>*************************<br><br>Multi-millionaire heiress <b>Layana Fairmont</b> was born with everything: she had wealth &amp; connections and was expected to become a trophy wife. Instead, she decides to take fate with her own hands and uses her inheritance to start a new life, one that didn’t constantly revolve around the privileged and wealthy. She also works at the Homeless Youth of America (HYA) and has a deep, abiding love for these children.<br><br>At one of the charity fundraises for HYA, Lana meets genius inventor <b>Brant Sharp.</b> Cool, calm, and collected, Brant became a tech billionaire at 20 years old and CEO of his own company. Lana and Brant have this immediate and insanely intense connection and though they’ve only spent one night together, both want more.<br><br>As their relationship blossoms and both secretly aware that their attraction is giving way to love, Lana comes across the ‘secret’ and all hopes for a happy future with Brant are shattered. Instead of breaking it off with him, Lana dives head-first into the mess and holds onto Brant, but still puts up a wall between them. And then she meets Lee.<br><br>Down-to-earth, flirtatious, and rough around the edges, <b>Lee</b> is a landscaper and the complete opposite of Brant. While Brant’s stoic, Lee is candid. Lee is fire, Brant is ice. And Lana loves both of them. She won’t give up Lee no matter what, setting off a plan of deceit, revenge, and betrayal to show just how far she’s willing to go to keep both men. <br><br>*************************<br><br>First I have to say, <b>
  <u>this is NOT a love triangle!!</u>
</b> Very hard to believe based on what I summarized before, but it’s true. Just go in with an open mind because this book is all about appearances. The stark truth lies beneath the façade. <br><br>Like I mentioned earlier, I thought the book premise was original. I didn’t figure out the big secret until 50 pages before it was revealed (I’m dumb, OK?) and when it was finally all out in the open, I was pretty much stunned speechless. But then, that secret also gave way to a ton of problems I had with the book.<br><br><b>1. Timelines.</b> I hate them. I hate them even more in books. I usually struggle with stories that are not set in the present and a good chunk of this book was from the past. <br><br><b>2. I had no connection to the characters.</b> Don’t get me wrong, I liked them but I never got used to the inner-monologues and the upper-class lifestyle – these are not very relatable characters. And because I didn’t find out the secret until the story was almost over, I spent most the book hating Lana’s guts and trying very hard not to smash my iPad against the wall. <br><br><b>3. The secret itself.</b> Okay, look. I have a terrible track record with books that revolve solely around this huge ass secret and then the secret turns out to be one lame excuse. Thankfully, that didn’t happen here. I actually admire the author for thinking of something so different. However, there is no way this secret would’ve worked in real life. I am a very logical and factual reader. 95% of the time logic wins over passion for me (unless the author is <i>really</i> good and wins over my emotions). And in this case, no emotions were evoked. This next part is a huge spoiler so only open it if you’ve read the book…<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
    <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[So Brant has DID. He somehow manages to be Lee, a grass-cutting landscaper for 2 years and no one recognized him as Brant, the genius inventor who graces the covers of dozens of magazines and social media?? Not just Lee, but how the heck does he pull off the 4 other personalities? Seriously confused here. I get that Brant himself would be confused but not other normal functioning people in society. I wish the author explained a bit more about that. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
   <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>4. The ending.</b> It was wrapped up too quickly, perfectly and became anti-climatic. <br><br>Not going to lie, this book gave me a massive headache. A big jumble of psychosis is what it is but I have to admit, it is unputdownable psychosis. Once I started, I didn’t stop reading until I was finished. This is a book that I would recommend solely for the shock factor. That’s it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409071760i/10929848._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>ARC provided by <u>Patchwork Press</u> via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14662198314200417053" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer795507057903516611"><b>LIVE!!!! <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Black-Lies-Alessandra-Torre-ebook/dp/B00N0EQM6Y/ref=pd_rhf_se_p_dnr_2'>http://www.amazon.com/Black-Lies-Ales...</a> </b><br/><br/><b>I wish I could give it a MILLION Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408968595i/10916079._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have thought about this book endlessly. I have thought about what I missed, how much I loved it, how heartbreaking it was, how many emotions I felt during such a short time. <br/><br/>Lastly, how do I put this epic book into words??<br/><br/>I will start at the beginning.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408968595i/10916080._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>We meet Layana, she is smart, beautiful, and independent. Growing up she was taught how to be the perfect wife. Despite being intelligent and excelling in sch</span>
  <span id="freeText795507057903516611" style="display:none"><b>LIVE!!!! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Black-Lies-Alessandra-Torre-ebook/dp/B00N0EQM6Y/ref=pd_rhf_se_p_dnr_2">http://www.amazon.com/Black-Lies-Ales...</a> </b><br><br><b>I wish I could give it a MILLION Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408968595i/10916079._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have thought about this book endlessly. I have thought about what I missed, how much I loved it, how heartbreaking it was, how many emotions I felt during such a short time. <br><br>Lastly, how do I put this epic book into words??<br><br>I will start at the beginning.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408968595i/10916080._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We meet Layana, she is smart, beautiful, and independent. Growing up she was taught how to be the perfect wife. Despite being intelligent and excelling in school her parents just want her to find a wealthy man from a good family to marry. Layana bides her time until she can leave her family and pursue her own life and passions. <br><br>Layana’s passion is helping the less fortunate. She works with a homeless shelter for kids. This is what brings her to meet Brant. Brant is a self-made billionaire tech genius. They meet and are both instantly attracted to each other. Brant is sexy, dedicated, smart, driven, and eccentric. Everything is going smoothly, they are the perfect couple. Brant even purposes to Layana, but she says no. Why?<br> <br>When Layana meets Lee, everything changes. Lee is a landscaper, barely getting by. He is also sexy as sin and rough around the edges. Something about Lee has Layana head over heels for him. While dating Brant, she pursues Lee for two years…she will stop at nothing to make him hers. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408968595i/10916081._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story will break your heart, it will have you questioning everything, it will have you screaming at your kindle, and texting your friends who have read it too demanding spoilers. <br><br><b>Whatever you do, don’t let anyone spoil this story for you, because no one can put this story into words for you and do it justice.</b> This story is EPIC, I just finished it last week and I already can’t wait to read it again. <br><br>It is no secret that I love Ms. Torre and I might be a <i>little</i> obsessed, and this story is just another reason why. <b>I highly recommend this book to everyone. It has everything: love, heartbreak, mystery, depth, and sexiness…yes and in Torre fashion it is hot as fuck!</b><br><br>I could go on and on about how awesome this story is and why you should read it, but I won’t because you need to be one clicking this and starting it ASAP!!<br><br><b>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3601944435" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7718449018676008346"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>I figured what the twist was before I started reading, so I think that changed the reading experience a bit more than if I had read this right when it came out and before I had read a few vague reviews. Even though they were spoiler free, they made it clear that this wasn't your typical romance....so I knew something was afoot before I started and my hypothesis was right. <br/><br/>Still, I enjoyed the story well enough. A super solid way to spend a <s>hungover</s> lazy Sunday afternoon. <br/><br/></span>

<div id="review_1058467595" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1058467595" />
    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1058467595?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Cristina Monica by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=secrets">secrets</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1058467595" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3215555548107194527"><blockquote>
  <strong>Love. It makes us do crazy things.</strong>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414387631ra/11647495.gif' width='500' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After seeing so many of my trust-worthy friends raving and raving about this book, I could not get it out of my mind. Even though I may not have read it right after being convinced by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1002402634?book_show_action=false&page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Patty’s great review</a>, I kept thinking about it and mentally planned – or at least tried to – for the perfect time to enjoy it, since I believed it would be dark.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <strong>Go ahead. Judge me. You have no idea what my love entails.</strong>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <strong>I love two men. I fuck two men.</strong>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <strong>If you </strong></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText3215555548107194527" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <strong>Love. It makes us do crazy things.</strong>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414387631ra/11647495.gif" width="500" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After seeing so many of my trust-worthy friends raving and raving about this book, I could not get it out of my mind. Even though I may not have read it right after being convinced by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1002402634?book_show_action=false&amp;page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Patty’s great review</a>, I kept thinking about it and mentally planned – or at least tried to – for the perfect time to enjoy it, since I believed it would be dark.<br><br><blockquote>
  <strong>Go ahead. Judge me. You have no idea what my love entails.</strong>
  <br>
  <br>
  <strong>I love two men. I fuck two men.</strong>
  <br>
  <br>
  <strong>If you think you’ve heard this story before, you haven’t.</strong>
</blockquote><br><br>I had no prejudices before starting this read. Sure, Layana does love two men and that frankly is not something I may actually and truthfully <em>approve</em> in real life, but I certainly was open to hear her side of the story and how it all stared.<br><br>I must say that, while it did not disappoint, I was patiently waiting for more.<br><blockquote>
  <strong>I turned, naked, save my underwear, and cast a mischievous smile toward his clothes.</strong>
  <br>
  <br>
  <strong>‘‘Strip’em.’’</strong>
  <br>
  <br>
  <strong>‘‘You do it.’’ A challenge and order in the tone.</strong>
  <br>
  <br>
  <strong>I shook my head. ‘‘I’ve got to break you of the habit of ordering women around.’’</strong>
</blockquote><br>Just from the start, when she meets Brant, whom is a very important character to the story, I found that there was missing something. A sparkle…Their way of meeting was not outstanding or completely taking us by surprise. Instead, it was a setting that was fitting the plot, yet did nothing to help me love the love-interest from the very beginning. But I did grow fond of him, as the story unfolded itself.<br><br>Layana is a bad – more like conflicted – girl. Or so I thought for most of the story.<br><blockquote>
  <strong>I know you don’t understand. I know you hate me. But you will soon find out Brant’s secret. I can’t keep it inside. It won’t stay quiet, is screaming silently until the plug is pulled and its howl will fill the air. And once you find out, you will understand. You would have done the same thing.</strong>
</blockquote><br>The fact that she was an honest person – except for the ‘secret’ that she kept postponing and postponing and postponing, trying to build suspense and interest, I imagine, but backfired because I started to feel annoyed after some time – helped me understand her better and especially her motives as to why she ‘cheated’ on her soon-to-be-fiancé that she loved with all her heart.<br><br>The sex wasn’t very explicitly long, which quite surprised me – but not in a negative way – for this<em> is</em> an adult contemporary romance. There was enough of it though, so the fact that it was not always ‘fire burning’ was not a problem itself.<br><br>What I did find to be a weakness though was the lack of characters in this story. There were very few of them! Or, if there were some, they were not present enough to be anything but cameos. Really forgettable ones. Which is a shame, because this author definitely knows how to create main characters we will want to read about…except for Lee, the<em> other</em> guy.<br><br>He just clearly did not care about Layana and only wanted sex. And sex. And sex again. And she fell for him and his care freeness. Even when things turn out to be different, I still was not convinced by everything he uttered.<br><br>The suspense was good, but it did get overwhelming. The romance was cute, but not always sigh-worthy. The writing fantastic, the atmosphere noticeable and rightly adding some complementary effect to the story. The plot did get repetitive from time to time, but was overall well-done.<br><br>It is worth reading, which is something I have to admit. There though effectively were scenes I would change to make this whole story more addictive and, really, there should have been more clues or twists as for what Brant’s secret is. <br><br>Happy reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3215555548107194527" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time"><img alt="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365526640p2/13070326.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1038910522?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=read-to-review-arc">read-to-review-arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=everyone-else-loves-it">everyone-else-loves-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=addiction-or-mental-disorders">addiction-or-mental-disorders</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1038910522" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14496774533022307554">*2.5 stars* <br/> <br/><b>**Spoiler-free review**</b><br/><br/>I can tell you already that 90% of readers are going to love this book. Like <i>loooooove</i> it and put it on their all-time favorites list. <br/><br/>Do you want to know a quick trick to see if you are going to be one of them?<br/><br/><b>Here are the questions to ask yourself: Do you like soap operas? Do you adore harlequin romances? Do you consider an "awesome twist" to be finding out that the man you've been seeing is your long lost 1/2 brother or that the baby you gave up for adoptio</b></span>
  <span id="freeText14496774533022307554" style="display:none">*2.5 stars* <br /> <br /><b>**Spoiler-free review**</b><br /><br />I can tell you already that 90% of readers are going to love this book. Like <i>loooooove</i> it and put it on their all-time favorites list. <br /><br />Do you want to know a quick trick to see if you are going to be one of them?<br /><br /><b>Here are the questions to ask yourself: Do you like soap operas? Do you adore harlequin romances? Do you consider an "awesome twist" to be finding out that the man you've been seeing is your long lost 1/2 brother or that the baby you gave up for adoption is your arch nemesis?<br /><br />If the answer to those questions is "yes," then you will love this book.</b><br /><br />It is no secret that this book has a large twist. Any review will say that. I certainly won't be giving anything away on that front. However, if you haven't caught on to the secret by the time the twist is revealed at 70%, then you somehow missed the ENORMOUS number of clues that the author dropped throughout the story. I'm not the most observant person in the world, but even I knew what the entire story was about by 15% in, and so it was almost painful to read the next 50%, knowing we are supposed to be in the dark. <br /><br />What bothered me the most about this story was the shear improbably of it. I mean, if you really think about the logistics of the story, it makes no sense. You'll know what I'm talking about when you get that far. It is just bananas that anyone would think this was realistic. <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[For real, this is a HUGE spoiler<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I find it impossible to believe that someone as visible and rich as Brant, who is compared to Bill Gates but is one of the most handsome and eligible bachelors, would be able to have an alter-ego that no one recognizes. How did the bartender, clients, ANYONE not know who he was?? It is like JFK Jr. mowing your lawn! <br /><br />How did Lee get a phone and apartment? How did he get a car and drivers license? How did he get dressed and not look in the mirror? How did he have a business if he was never around??<br /><br />Why didn't Lana do some research into the disease? Why didn't she consult Drs before deciding to keep Brant and Lee in the dark for years? It was beyond strange to me. <br /><br />For me, it felt as dramatic and silly as a soap opera. It was one of those DA DA DA!--&gt; He has a split personality!! that I see on TV.<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I also RAGED at the fact that Lana had unprotected sex with Brant and Lee. Moronic much, Lana?<br /><br />While I wanted to give the premise of the book 1 or 2 stars, I almost ended up rounding up to three stars because of the little creepings of emotion that I felt for these characters. I have to admit, Lee wormed his way into my heart a bit, despite my knowing how manipulative and silly this book was. The writing was also competent, though I didn't get all hot and bothered over the sex scenes. <br /><br />Moral of the story is that you could do a lot worse in the world of M/F contemporary romance, but that didn't make me like this story any more. I couldn't get over how dramatic, improbable, and soap-opera-ish this book was. However, if you like far-fetched, interesting stories, this one just might work for you.<br /><br />*ARC provided in exchange for an honest review*</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9226932230892414846"><br/><b><a href='http://video214.com/play/xymTaB3uunuRdtEhEYxSHw/s/dark' rel='nofollow noopener'>'Black Lies' mini-trailer</a><br/><br/><br/>This review will be even worst than my usual non-review review because I can't even review this book properly without giving away things that make it so great so I am going to say this:<br/><br/><br/>I only really need two things in a book in order for me to enjoy it: <br/><br/>1. I want the story to be original. I did enjoy a tween billionaire deflower a virgin once (twice, actually) but that was then and this is now. Give me something new, OK? <br/><br/>2. I want that original story I mentioned above ma</b></span>
  <span id="freeText9226932230892414846" style="display:none"><br /><b><a href="http://video214.com/play/xymTaB3uunuRdtEhEYxSHw/s/dark" rel="nofollow noopener">'Black Lies' mini-trailer</a><br /><br /><br />This review will be even worst than my usual non-review review because I can't even review this book properly without giving away things that make it so great so I am going to say this:<br /><br /><br />I only really need two things in a book in order for me to enjoy it: <br /><br />1. I want the story to be original. I did enjoy a tween billionaire deflower a virgin once (twice, actually) but that was then and this is now. Give me something new, OK? <br /><br />2. I want that original story I mentioned above make me feel. Something. Happy. Sad. Horny. Angry. Anything. <br /><br />Simple, right? Right. <br /><br />When I pick up a book, any book, by Alessadra Torre, I KNOW 100% without a doubt that I am going to get both.<br /><br />I always describe Alessandra's writing to my friends like this: when I read her books, I feel as if I'm having a grown up slumber party with one of my best friends where she tells me about her naughty, exciting life and leaves nothing out. I feel so at ease reading her stories that half the time I don't realize it's after 4am and I should have gone to bed HOURS ago yet I am so lost in a book that I am still awake and I don't care if I am comatose the next morning because some books are worth losing sleep over. <br /><br />Long story short - I really enjoy Alessandra's writing.<br /><br />This book is no different. Great story that sucked <i><u>me</u></i> in right from the prologue, plot twists, hot sex (very few write sex as well as Alessandra does, IMO) and then 'THE SECRET'!!! If you are in the mood for something that's clever, <u>original</u>, well written, sexy as hell, has hot men and even hotter rides (come on ... I don't know of anyone other than myself who's even heard of Land Rover Defender! I love a girl who appreciates all that horse power. *virtual high five, AT*), this is a book for you. I can definitely see myself rereading this one in not so distant future so I can finally pick up on all those clues I missed as I devoured this story first time around.<br /><br />See, I told you this review review will stink, didn't I?<br /><br />Cheers!<br /><br />P.S. I am not ashamed to admit it - I didn't guess the 'BIG SECRET' until she spelled it out for me in black and white towards the end.<br /><br />P.P.S. I know the epilogue left this wide open for a sequel but I don't know if I want one. <br /><br />P.P.P.S. Yes, I think I do want that sequel after all.</b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1003065099" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9701290301027957560"><b>5 Stars and More Stars<br/>* * * * * <i> Spoiler Free FREE! </i><br/>How many times have you wished the person you love could be more like someone else you knew in your past… you love the man you are with now… you understand him… you are drawn to him… things are good… even better than good… and yet… there is something else… which would make it perfect…<br/><br/>This wondering about what we would do for love… what extremes we would go to is nothing new… yet in the hands of Alessandra Torre… we are taken on a journey which </b></span>
  <span id="freeText9701290301027957560" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars and More Stars<br>* * * * * <i> Spoiler Free FREE! </i><br>How many times have you wished the person you love could be more like someone else you knew in your past… you love the man you are with now… you understand him… you are drawn to him… things are good… even better than good… and yet… there is something else… which would make it perfect…<br><br>This wondering about what we would do for love… what extremes we would go to is nothing new… yet in the hands of Alessandra Torre… we are taken on a journey which never travels a straight line. The crafting of the tale … the lure of understanding what is happening… these things draw you into her web and you are held precariously… for every time you think you know what is happening… you are flipped until she decides it is time to take everything in…. </b><br><br>All of our characters are multi dimensional… no one and nothing is as it appears… why our people do what they do cannot be discussed… only experienced.<br><br>If we are lucky in life, we experience full blown…dedicated love for another… we give ourselves over to this… we sometimes do questionable things… and it can be a risk… This type of love demands trust… sometimes sacrifice and balls of steel.<br><br>Black Lies touches on all of this and more…. and the more is all Alessandra Torre. <br><br><i>Advanced kindly provided by the author</i><br> <br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1586446543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11727253803636640609"><b>4.5 'Black Lies and a Secret' Stars!</b><br/><i>BR with my Shhluts :D - Read as part of the ShhLYT(F)BR week on Dark Books.</i><br/><a href='http://s196.photobucket.com/user/Albyz92/media/Collages%20Goodreads/Black%20Lies%20-%20Alessandra%20Torre_zpsmgws0pth.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458814647i/18533186.png' alt=' photo Black Lies - Alessandra Torre_zpsmgws0pth.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Honestly, I don't even know where to start with this review. Two days after finishing this and I am still blown away by the amazing talent Alessandra Torre has. I have read <i>Black Lies</i> as part of this week's TopPick on the Shh... group on Dark Books (you can still join us!) and I knew I was getting myself into something different, something I haven't read before. And boy was I right!</span>
  <span id="freeText11727253803636640609" style="display:none"><b>4.5 'Black Lies and a Secret' Stars!</b><br><i>BR with my Shhluts :D - Read as part of the ShhLYT(F)BR week on Dark Books.</i><br><a href="http://s196.photobucket.com/user/Albyz92/media/Collages%20Goodreads/Black%20Lies%20-%20Alessandra%20Torre_zpsmgws0pth.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458814647i/18533186.png" alt=" photo Black Lies - Alessandra Torre_zpsmgws0pth.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Honestly, I don't even know where to start with this review. Two days after finishing this and I am still blown away by the amazing talent Alessandra Torre has. I have read <i>Black Lies</i> as part of this week's TopPick on the Shh... group on Dark Books (you can still join us!) and I knew I was getting myself into something different, something I haven't read before. And boy was I right! It was that and so much more.. Thank you Shhluts for recommending this to me!<br><br>Torre starts the first part of the novel with: <i>“This is a love story, but not one that is easy to read.”</i> It definitely is that, for sure! <i>Black Lies</i> is a love story between three characters: Layana 'Lana' Fairmont a.k.a Lucky (a young heiress who has just recieved her trust fund and wants to enjoy it), Brant Sharp (the hot CEO of a tech multi-million company and benefactor of the charity Lana works in) and Lee (a sexy landscaper that Lana cannot stop herself from wanting).<br><br><i>
  <b>Go ahead. Judge me. You have no idea what my love entails.<br>I love two men. I fuck two men. <br>If you think you’ve heard this story before, you haven’t.</b>
</i><br><br>I believe I will say what everyone says about this book but let me just tell you something: I hate love triangles and I hate cheating and I still LOVED this book. This is not a typical love story. If you are curious and you want to read <i>Black Lies</i> GO BLIND. Do not look for spoilers, it will totally ruin the experience for you. Keep an open mind and do not judge what happens until you finish it! Trust me and all the other reviewers that have said this, you will not regret it. <br><br><i>
  <b>When you really love someone, you cannot walk away. No matter what they do. No matter the lies from their mouth, or the actions from their bodies, you tie yourself tightly to their sail and vow to be there through thick and thin. Let the wind blow you where it may. Even if that place is a crash. Even if that place tears you apart and kills anything good.</b>
</i><br><br>Alessandra, I am at your feet. This book messed up with my head, BIG TIME. And I loved it. This is pure Torre's writing style, raw and beautiful on its own. The words flow and you cannot stop but continue reading the story (even though it makes you hate the characters sometimes). AT has created three outstanding characters: they are super-complex, with amazing deepth and she will make you fall in love with all of them. She will make you fall in love with this wonderful love story.<br><br><i>
  <b>I love her completely. She returns the love wildly. This love is worth the unsaid truths. The hidden lies.<br><br>“I don’t love you despite this. I love you, including this. Every part of you, even parts you don’t know.”</b>
</i><br><br>And this novel will make you feel hot, like OFF-THE-CHARTS HOT. The sex scenes are out of this world, they are exquisitely written and extremily fresh and intense. The chemistry between the characters is superb and it will make you feel every freaking thing. It's a mindfuck, it's a roller coaster of emotions. Especially after the big twist, when you discover 'the secret'. You want to know this secret? READ THE BOOK. Seriously. I will not tell you ;)<br><br><i>
  <b>He gripped my hair when he thrust into me. Moaned my name when he turned me over and took me from behind. He made me come with his cock, then his fingers, then his mouth, before pounding a rhythm into me that I would never forget.<br><br>‘It was worth it as soon as I saw you’.</b>
</i><br><br>Therefore, my rating for <i>Black Lies</i> is 4.5 STARS because I know this book will stay forever with me, it just made me feel every emotion possible and I loved it. Sometimes it was even too much for me to handle so that is why I haven't rate it with 5 stars (maybe some of you know that I am not always ready to dig into dark romance books), I still have book hangover lol However, I have to say: if you haven't read this book, if you are afraid to check it out (like I was), even if you hate love triangles and cheating, please, GIVE THIS BOOK A CHANCE because I am pretty sure that if you finish it you will not regret the experience. I totally recommend!<br><br><b>CHECK OUT MY BLOG HERE:</b><br><a href="https://albaandhersecrets.wordpress.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447323775i/16986965.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11727253803636640609" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1146036876" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1146036876" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1146036876?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=is-getting-hot-in-here">is-getting-hot-in-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=i-must-like-mind-torture">i-must-like-mind-torture</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=filthy-billionaires">filthy-billionaires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=the-alpha-syndrome">the-alpha-syndrome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=oh-the-angst">oh-the-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=ride-the-drama-llama">ride-the-drama-llama</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1146036876" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14963514364940336253"><b>4,5 Mind blown Stars. </b>	<br/><br/>I will not tell you much about this story, not only because the blurb says pretty much all, but also because everything I can say can spoil the story. <br/>Lana is in love with Grant, the sexy tech billionaire who wants to marry her. But she is also in a relationship with Lee, the sexy garden. <br/>Don’t make assumptions, don’t judge. This is one story so complex and so full of lies that only a strong an indestructible love can save them. But which “them” will it save?<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419980184i/13152079.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book mak</span>
  <span id="freeText14963514364940336253" style="display:none"><b>4,5 Mind blown Stars. </b>	<br><br>I will not tell you much about this story, not only because the blurb says pretty much all, but also because everything I can say can spoil the story. <br>Lana is in love with Grant, the sexy tech billionaire who wants to marry her. But she is also in a relationship with Lee, the sexy garden. <br>Don’t make assumptions, don’t judge. This is one story so complex and so full of lies that only a strong an indestructible love can save them. But which “them” will it save?<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419980184i/13152079.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book makes you leave so far out of your comfort zone, that you will even forget what comfort means anymore. This isn’t just a book, it’s a reading experience. It’s angsty, raw, emotional and will leave you asking “what the heck is going on here” for most of the time. <br>I don’t know if it was pretty predictable but I figured out what was going on around 30%, so when the plot was uncovered it only confirmed my suspicions, but however, it was an amazing experience, very well written that sucked me in in the begging. This is, without a doubt, one of those unforgettable readings that will be burned in my memory indefinitely.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4,5 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b>	Lana was one of the most complexes heroines ever written. You will hate her, you will despise her actions, but you will also love her and admire her strength and perseverance. In the end, I loved her. Lee and Brant are completely opposites, one is cold ice, and the other is fire hot. One is a sweet billionaire, the other is a sexy gardener. However, you will fall for both of them and even when it’s clear which one she will end with, you will certainly miss the other. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Mental Disorders.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14963514364940336253" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5426879322450131396">4--<b>Crazy</b>--Stars!!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408980211ra/10917050.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It's impossible to review this book and not give anything away. This was classic Alessandra Torre. Seriously, how this woman comes up with this stuff.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393538960ra/8728928.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>For me this book was just plain weird.   <span id="freeText5426879322450131396" style="display:none">4--<b>Crazy</b>--Stars!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408980211ra/10917050.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's impossible to review this book and not give anything away. This was classic Alessandra Torre. Seriously, how this woman comes up with this stuff.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393538960ra/8728928.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For me this book was just plain weird. Intriguing weird though. I figured things out pretty quick, and how it all played out was half the fun. <br><br>Literally, the whole book I was going<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436556ra/882356.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The whole story was just plain crazy. Like is this even possible crazy? And does it even matter because I was seriously glued to the book and read it in one sitting. <br><br>I'm not even sure it was a romance. Sure, there was some in there but I think the biggest thing was all of the WTF moments and how Alessandra Torre was able to pull a story like this off. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395983272ra/9072409.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, this type of book is not something I gravitate towards. But it does make me question what's going on in that head of hers....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408980211ra/10917051.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I think everyone should read this one simply for the wow factor that comes in creating such a unique, intriguing, addicting story. </span>

<div id="review_968465980" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/968465980" />
    <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady"><img alt="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370640721p2/14351108.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/968465980?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady">Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=all-time-favorites-series">all-time-favorites-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer968465980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11981271133087306414"><b>5 Million Stars</b><br/><br/>Completely spoiler free.....<br/><a href='http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/BlackLies2_zps36df2624.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408341492i/10838797._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo BlackLies2_zps36df2624.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I will begin this review by saying there is really no way to review this book. It is a mind zapping story. One that takes you on a bevy of emotions. You will swoon, you will sigh, you will love, you will hate, you will get angry, you will get befuddled, you will get perplexed, you will not understand and then <b>YOU - WILL - UNDERSTAND!!!!</b> For an author to take you on such an experience, who makes you think and contemplate your sanity and then brings y</span>
  <span id="freeText11981271133087306414" style="display:none"><b>5 Million Stars</b><br><br>Completely spoiler free.....<br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/BlackLies2_zps36df2624.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408341492i/10838797._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo BlackLies2_zps36df2624.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I will begin this review by saying there is really no way to review this book. It is a mind zapping story. One that takes you on a bevy of emotions. You will swoon, you will sigh, you will love, you will hate, you will get angry, you will get befuddled, you will get perplexed, you will not understand and then <b>YOU - WILL - UNDERSTAND!!!!</b> For an author to take you on such an experience, who makes you think and contemplate your sanity and then brings you around full circle is Extraordinary and Outstanding.<br><br>What I will tell you- There is Layana "Lana" Farmont, Brant Sharp, Lee and Jillian. The web that these 4 spin is intoxicating and mind altering. That is all you get, it is all you need. While reading I thought of this famous quote.....<br><b>Oh, what a tangled web we weave <br>When first we practice to deceive</b><br>The brilliance of this book is what your perceptions are at the beginning, the deceits throughout the book, followed up with the insanity of the truth = Book Perfection.<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/kiss5_zpsc5340fd5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408334167i/10838143.jpg" alt=" photo kiss5_zpsc5340fd5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story is passionate and consuming. It's about LOVE and what you will do to keep it. You sacrifice ALL in hopes of gaining EVERYTHING. It's a total mind altering experience. So much so that I reread the story once I had finished. Reading the second time around was such a different experience for I understood so much more about the characters. I was able to see nuisances that I had missed. It brought me to a deeper level, a much more emotional read than my first time. <br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/BlackLies_zpsb7e6e619.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408334167i/10838144.jpg" alt=" photo BlackLies_zpsb7e6e619.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I think everyone should go into this story somewhat blind- I would also recommend you read with a buddy. There are times when I had to seek friends who had read to bring me off the ceiling. I wasn't sure I was going to survive......The most important thing to remember is to continue reading, even when you want to throw your kindle against the wall, keep reading, when you think your hatred gets the best of you, keep reading, because in the end, you will be rewarded- I promise.<br><br>I have read all of Alessandra Torre's books. I can say that she has magic fingers. She can tell a story brilliantly. Her words come alive and evoke the strongest of emotions. She is a truly gifted and talented writer. You have a forever and ever fan in me.... <br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Gifs/BlowingAKiss_zps4a502d1e.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387150875ra/7540358.gif" alt=" photo BlowingAKiss_zps4a502d1e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>♥<i>ARC from the author in exchange for an honest review</i>♥<br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1027359262" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16621020975213363802"><b>LIVE</b> - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1vjRLA2'>http://amzn.to/1vjRLA2</a><br/><br/><br/><b>A refreshingly, brilliant book! </b><br/><br/>When I saw the cover and the genre (erotica) I automatically thought- a sex driven book. I was totally wrong! <br/><br/>My inner <b>emotional junkie</b> loved the mystery in this book. I loved coming up with all kinds of theories and having my friends neither deny or confirm my thoughts. Instead they just encouraged me to keep reading. I had the best time guessing and never knowing if I was right or wrong. Being an avid reader it's hard for me to truly</span>
  <span id="freeText16621020975213363802" style="display:none"><b>LIVE</b> - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1vjRLA2">http://amzn.to/1vjRLA2</a><br><br><br><b>A refreshingly, brilliant book! </b><br><br>When I saw the cover and the genre (erotica) I automatically thought- a sex driven book. I was totally wrong! <br><br>My inner <b>emotional junkie</b> loved the mystery in this book. I loved coming up with all kinds of theories and having my friends neither deny or confirm my thoughts. Instead they just encouraged me to keep reading. I had the best time guessing and never knowing if I was right or wrong. Being an avid reader it's hard for me to truly be surprised in a book because normally I can guess right away. <br><br><u>
  <b>READING ADVICE:</b>
</u><br><br>✣GO INTO THIS BOOK KNOWING NOTHING!<br>In life there aren't very many simple pleasures and when you can experience one it's best not to rob yourself of those moments. Allowing the suspense and mystery guide you through this book was a fun experience. Having those <b>aha moments</b> after the secret was revealed was so much fun.<br><br>✣ <b>But</b> even if you realize early on the “secret” and/or if you know before going into the book what the secret is, I still think you can have an enjoyable experience. <br><br>✣Either way my lips are sealed.✣<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388276420ra/7785614.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><blockquote> <b>”This is a love story, but not one that is easy to read.”</b>
</blockquote>For the last couple years I've picked some books that I wanted to re-read and read them to my husband when we go to bed. I've decided this is going to be one of those books that I read to him while we are snuggled up in bed. <br><br>Here's how I felt about the whole book.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409466713ra/10983024.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>PAY IT FORWARD</b>: BBU had a FB book contest and I won. I'm going to pay it forward and giveaway a copy too. To enter, follow this link -&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://on.fb.me/1ngV57e">http://on.fb.me/1ngV57e</a><br><br><b>Standalone</b><br><br>**Won this book from a Facebook contest hosted by <a href="https://www.facebook.com/BookBabesUnite/posts/831215806918787" rel="nofollow noopener">Book Babes Unite.</a> Thank you, Babes, for the book. **<br><br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408724793i/10887518.png" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IJyzNx2U5OzNYi+e7oudtPxh3HOFTFxIKUJ6uew7lwgautrlpsothGpJm/8ZfpdrKj47u0vB0i9yPDwIIXhlkg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZQI9ULp3JRGdGpNJyCgmLXxISJQ/4oYIaicx//fMK+1fJFSCASnseToxJyg/3SzyqhevXPFvCG8xWXdOOo/Zdw==')})
  }
//]]>
